  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5adafaa1-d546-4af4-9a62-66d0db5b3360'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

Now, she's back on track and looking forward to her new, quiet life. Until she meets the man of her dreams. The tattooed, muscled biker plies her with tequila-and the best sex of her life. She knows it isn't the tequila and hot sex talking. He's the kind of man she's always wanted. Unfortunately, he's also her new boss . . . <br /><br />Kane "Tack" Allen has a rule. He doesn't employ someone he's slept with. So when he learns he spent last night in bed with his new office manager, he quickly fires Tyra. Yet when Tyra stands up to him and fights for her job, Tack is intrigued. He tells her she can keep her job on one condition: no more sex. Ever. But as things heat up between them, Tack finds that he'll be the one breaking all the rules...</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer803529098" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17766852801157735250"><i>As I write this review, I’m wearing grey yoga pants. Well, they’re a darker grey on the outside and a much softer, lighter grey on the inside. They have a white drawstring, and while it’s not really necessary to tie it, I have it tied in a bow anyway. They’re really soft and comfortable, and they’re the kind of pants you could wear just around the house. But if you wanted, you could also wear them out to the grocery store or the mall or the gym or basically anywhere that wasn’t too dressy.<br/><br/>I’m al</i></span>
  <span id="freeText17766852801157735250" style="display:none"><i>As I write this review, I’m wearing grey yoga pants. Well, they’re a darker grey on the outside and a much softer, lighter grey on the inside. They have a white drawstring, and while it’s not really necessary to tie it, I have it tied in a bow anyway. They’re really soft and comfortable, and they’re the kind of pants you could wear just around the house. But if you wanted, you could also wear them out to the grocery store or the mall or the gym or basically anywhere that wasn’t too dressy.<br /><br />I’m also wearing a pink and white cotton henley. It has small stripes, not the big fat ones. And they’re horizontal and not vertical. The shirt also has ruffles at the neck along with four white buttons. It has long sleeves that go just to my wrists. I hate sleeves that hang over my hands unless it’s like a fleece hoodie and I’m outside and my hands are cold. Then I like it when the sleeves hang over my hands.<br /><br />My bra is a beige and cotton, but it’s not really a basic bra. It’s a balconette bra with just a little light padding in the bottom of the cups. I generally need a padded bra because my boobs are definitely on the larger side and I need the extra support. And I also need the padding because it’s cold out right now and when it gets this cold, my nipples get hard and show through my shirt. And my panties are also beige, but they’re not cotton. They’re that microfiber kind that looks seamless under your pants. And since my yoga pants are kind of thin, I don’t want a VPL. For those of you who don’t know what that is, it’s a visible panty line.<br /><br />Anyway, I think I look pretty cute for a Saturday where I’m just hanging out at home and catching up on a few things.</i><br /><br /><br />If you liked the detailed description of what I’m wearing, Motorcycle Man is definitely the book for you. In fact, I’m pretty sure that more than a quarter of the book could have been edited out because it’s full of endless paragraphs detailing stupid shit like what the heroine is wearing or what they cooked and ate for breakfast, lunch, and dinner.<br /><br />Also, if you don’t have any attachments to correct grammar and punctuation, this could also be the book for you. Honestly, I think that Kristen Ashley just throws commas in sentences randomly because she’s unsure where they truly go. And she obviously doesn’t have an editor. And if she <i>does</i> have an editor, that person should be fired immediately for incompetence.<br /><br />I know it seems like I’m nit-picking a lot of things here, but come on… I expected more than this form a book that rated in the high fours on Amazon and goodreads.<br /><br />I will talk about the story, though.<br /><br />Kane “Tack” Allen is our hero. If you want to call him that. I’m personally going to call him a sexist, misogynistic, abusive asshole. He is one of many “heroes” in this new trend where authors try to pass abuse off as sexy. <br /><br />You know what’s sexy? A man who views a woman as his equal and treats her as such. A man who thinks that, in spite of her vagina, she has valid ideas, thoughts, and opinions.<br /><br />You know what’s not sexy? A man who tells a woman that there are some things she's just going to have accept, and some things she just doesn't get to know or have an opinion about because she's a woman. That infidelity happens and you just need to let it go because it’s none of your business, and this is just the way it is in his world.<br /><br />Well, fuck that.<br /><br />And fuck him.<br /><br />Because we all live in the same world, asshole. <br /><br />Ugh.<br /><br />Here’s another thing: Tack has a tendency to grab the heroine, Tyra, around the neck and push her up against walls. Now, grabbing someone’s neck when they’ve give you permission to do so because they find it sexy is one thing, but doing it while the woman is basically crying and cowering and asking him to stop is altogether something different. You know what they call that? Assault. And the author tries to explain this behavior away by having Tack tell Tyra he’s doing it because he wants to "feel her pulse." Because he’s so overwhelmed with the need to know she’s okay and breathing with a beating heart.<br /><br />Umm…<br /><br />You know how you can tell if a woman is breathing and her heart is beating? You fucking ask her. If she's standing up and talking, she's probably breathing just fine.<br /><br />This behavior is not sexy, ladies. This behavior, and our acceptance of it, is what has led to the rape-culture we are currently dealing with as a society.<br /><br />I love a dominating alpha hero. They are my favorite. But everything needs to be consensual. No means no. There are some authors who understand this and write alpha males I totally dig, and totally want to bang. Unfortunately, Kristen Ashley misses the mark on this. <br /><br />Motorcycle Man was not for me.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17766852801157735250" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

</a><br><br><b>5+++++ stars.<br><br>Holy smokes! *kissing my Kindle…again* Fan-freakin-tastic!</b> Tack sure gave Tate a run for his money! God, the man has a way to lay it all out…he is incredibly swoonalicious and <i>hawt</i> as all get out! Yeah, handsome, I’m kissing you from head to toes. Well, sometimes you’re a jerk. But you’re my wonderful jerk and I wouldn’t expect anything less from a man like you. That said, Tack made it all up to me when the scary biker dude who is full of his very own brand of badassness reveals his super gentle, sweet and kind side. I adore it when his eyes get so soft and warm. Imagine, he even loves to cuddle with his old lady. *Le sigh* Yeah, Tack shines—sweet, scary biker sunbeams, ladies! The dialogue they’re dishing out at each other is A.W.E.S.O.M.E.!! They sure gave one another a piece of their minds on a regular basis. I cannot count how many great quotes I found in this book. Too many…Well, I think most of the readers will experience a collective delirium of joy while reading MM. I adored the pulse thingie—it was super cute and so thoughtful, Tack!<br><br>Even though I don’t want to complain I felt that Tyra is saying “we’re over” a little too often. Every time they hit a rough patch, she gives up and declares that she wants out. Too easy, my lovely! It’s good to know that Tack didn’t let her walk out on him though. Gosh, the woman is throwing sass! Come to think of it, both of them have a serious case of attitude. Tack brought so much color, passion and love into Tyra's life that after tasting something very special, she didn't want to settle for anything less, not anything less than perfect. <br><br><i>”The ride is not over but if I can keep my Club together and find a sweet, feisty woman who’s got my back and enough to her that she’ll stay there, holding me up not dragging me down, I figure I’d find my way to beauty eventually. And I’d find absolution because I’d know, I earned the love of that woman, a woman who’s got so much to her it’ll take years to dig down and find the heart of her, that would be my reward.”</i><br><br>MM starts off with Tyra Masters having "found" the right guy. He was the one. The motorcycle man in bed with her was the man of her dreams. Living, breathing, gorgeous, tattooed, gravelly-voiced, great with his hands, mouth and other parts of his spectacular anatomy proof that she was absolutely right. BTW, I added the word "spectacular" myself. *wiggling eyebrows* Usually Tyra doesn't jump into bed with men she barely knew. Well, a little surprise lies ahead of you, my dear.<br><br><i>"Close the door on your way out, would you, Red?"</i><br><br>Tyra is 35, well organized, sensible and loves to drink rejuvenating green tea. Her life is about to get a bit messy when she starts a new job as an office manager. Ride Custom Bars and Bikes is Tyra's new place of employment. Chaos Motorcycle Club is the owner of the very famous garage, and Tack (Kane) Allen is the president of CMC and Tyra's new boss all at the same time. Why oh why did I get this feeling…been there, done that when the scary biker dude said such "nice" things to Tyra:<br><br><i>"I do not work with bitches who've had my dick in their mouth."<br>(…) "I do not fuck anyone who's got my signature on their paycheck."<br>(…) "Darlin' you're the greediest piece of ass I've had in my bed in a long fuckin' time. I got a taste for greedy, you think I'm not gonna take it?</i><br><br>Ah yes, it dawns on me…a certain...Tate…Jackson…Sweet Dreams?<br><br>Boy, they gave one another lip. I loved Tack’s sexy as hell grin! Scary Tack gave her a fair warning and when he wants something he gets it. Game on! <br><br><i>"Red," he said softly. "You entered the game, it's my game, babe, you play it my way."</i><br><br><b>YOWZA!<br><br>Kristen's stories are such an indulgence, and you don't indulge every day. If you did, it wouldn't be an indulgence anymore. It's like expensive chocolate that's melting on your tongue. I don't eat it every day either.<br><br>The epilogue</b><br>One word: epic<br><br><i>”Truth, honesty, perseverance, strength, love of all kinds and forgiveness are all beautiful, Tack. The most beautiful stories ever told are the most difficult to take.”</i><br><br><br>P.S.<br>Tabby and Shy’s story will be told! Wooohooo! I’m sooo excited! Thank you, Kristen! *smooches* my lovely!<br><br><b>P.P.S.<br>I'm sorry, Tack, but Tate stays above and beyond. You did not knock him off his pedestal.</b><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1894914639421598768"><b>5 STARS!!!</b><br/><br/>Wow! What a fantastic ending to a fabulous book and series! <br/><br/>I just finished this story, have tears in my eyes, and I'm not able to wait until tomorrow (when I return home) to write my review. I wish I had the time and money (dang cruise ship wi-fi charges) to write the review this book deserves. Unfortunately, I don't.   <span id="freeText1894914639421598768" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS!!!</b><br /><br />Wow! What a fantastic ending to a fabulous book and series! <br /><br />I just finished this story, have tears in my eyes, and I'm not able to wait until tomorrow (when I return home) to write my review. I wish I had the time and money (dang cruise ship wi-fi charges) to write the review this book deserves. Unfortunately, I don't. However, I can express my love for this story, it's amazing characters, and it's fantastic epilogue. Tack and Tyra are my favorite couple in this series, and I loved their arduous yet heartwarming romance. <br /><br />This is my favorite conversation between Tack and Tyra. It's just so them. It's priceless. <br /><br /><i>"It goes like this," I began to explain. "We get to know each other. We have a huge-ass wedding. We spend time just us and, um... Tab and Rush, of course. Then we start on a family."<br />   "Got it all scheduled," he noted. <br />   "Yes," I retuned. <br />   "What's a huge-ass wedding?"<br />   "Don't ask that," I advised. "Just show up."<br />   His grin turned wicked and I liked it. That was, I liked it until he enquired, "You askin' me to marry you, Red?"<br />   I wasn't even sipping coffee and, still,  I choked. <br />   Then I pushed out, "What?"<br />   "I accept"<br />   I shook my head and kept shaking it when I requested clarification, "Let me get this straight. Did you just accept my non-marriage offer?" <br />   "Non-marriage?"<br />   "I didn't ask!" My voice was rising. <br />   "So you just wanna shack up?" he asked but didn't wait on my answer. "I'm good with that too."<br />  Gah!<br />   "I'm getting my huge-ass wedding," I declared. <br />   "So you <i>are</i> askin' me to marry you," he noted. <br />   Gah! Gah! Gah!<br />   Sharp as a tack.</i><br /><br />Note: A special shout-out to Michele. Thank you so much for your thoughtfulness and generosity. You made my trip even better! <br /><br /><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</i></span>

<div id="review_334758159" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/334758159" />
    <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish"><img alt="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1398981306p2/1113032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/334758159?book_show_action=true">May 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" class="user" itemprop="url" name="UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish" href="/user/show/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish">UniquelyMoi ~ BlithelyBookish</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=author-kristen-ashley">author-kristen-ashley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=series-dream-man">series-dream-man</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=ebook-own-have-read">ebook-own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=5-stars-or-higher">5-stars-or-higher</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=badass-biker-dudes">badass-biker-dudes</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=2012-reads">2012-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=top-heroines">top-heroines</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=im-a-kristen-ashley-ho">im-a-kristen-ashley-ho</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=top-10-heroes">top-10-heroes</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer334758159" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1775895521168456833"><br/><b> 5+++++++ stars</b><blockquote>“Truth, honesty, perseverance, strength, love of all kinds and forgiveness are all beautiful, Tack. The most beautiful stories ever told are the most difficult to take.”</blockquote>You should probably just go buy the book and read <i>it</i> instead of wasting your time reading this review, because I really don’t know how to express what I am feeling about this story or the man, Kane “Tack” Allen. I was left deeply, completely, emotionally sated… and yet empty, too, because once it ended… I was lost.</span>
  <span id="freeText1775895521168456833" style="display:none"><br /><b> 5+++++++ stars</b><blockquote>“Truth, honesty, perseverance, strength, love of all kinds and forgiveness are all beautiful, Tack. The most beautiful stories ever told are the most difficult to take.”</blockquote>You should probably just go buy the book and read <i>it</i> instead of wasting your time reading this review, because I really don’t know how to express what I am feeling about this story or the man, Kane “Tack” Allen. I was left deeply, completely, emotionally sated… and yet empty, too, because once it ended… I was lost. I was just… <i>lost.</i><br /><br />And, you know, I actually cried because it ended. Not <i>because</i> of the ending, even though it was incredibly emotional. I didn’t cry because the book was too short, even though it was, but had it been 1,000,003 pages it <i>still</i> would have been too short. The tears were not because it was sad, though there were some heartbreaking scenes and I did cry for those, and tears of joy for the happy scenes, too… but honest to God, I cried because it was over. Because there was no more… I don’t think that’s ever happened to me before.<br /><br />*sigh* <br /><br /><b>Okay, about Tack and Tyra - </b><br /><br />Tyra is awesome. Just awesome. She's fun, strong, independent, loving, compassionate. She's kick-ass, take no prisoners, protective and .... yeah, awesome. The perfect heroine for a bad-ass biker dude.<br /><br /><b>And speaking of bad-ass biker dudes...</b> this story is loaded with them, from start to finish, but since this is Tack's story...<br /><br />Tack is obnoxious, intense, crass, rude, brutal, harsh, foul mouthed and short tempered, arrogant… and even though he’s all those things, he’s also honorable, loving, compassionate, determined, sex in the flesh, funny, easy going, understanding… Sure, he’s done some shitty things but he’s also this man:<blockquote>“Okay,” I said softly. “So this was why I got all those ‘laters’? Because you weren’t fired up to share all of this?”<br /><br />“This was why,” he confirmed.<br /><br />I pulled in breath through my nose.<br /><br />Before I could process any of what he said much less come to terms with it, Tack stated, “Love and redemption.”<br /><br />My head tipped on the pillow. “What?”<br /><br />“That movie you made me watch, first time at your house. Love and redemption. You said, ‘the most beautiful stories ever told are the most difficult to take’. You said that, Red. Right out. And I knew if you got that, when it was later and I shared my shit with you, you’d get me. I never thought my story was beautiful. I thought it was shit. But you said that and when you did, I saw it. The ride is not over but if I can keep my Club together and find a sweet, feisty woman who’s got my back and enough to her that she’ll stay there, holding me up not dragging me down, I figure I’d find my way to beauty eventually. And I’d find absolution because I’d know, I earned the love of that woman, a woman who’s got so much to her it’ll take years to dig down and find the heart of her, that would be my reward.”</blockquote> And it's this vulnerability, his understanding of not just who is he, but who he wants to be...this is why I love Tack and this story, and why he’s become my favorite Kristen Ashley hero, and why <i>you</i> need to get this book, read this book then pimp this book to everyone you know! Now.<br /><br />-----<br />If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1775895521168456833" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/381179285" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/381179285?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer381179285" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4350900457782063057"><b>5 Hawt and Handsome Tack Stars </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/123b2f7e-cb78-4a11-bd8c-0e04d6479c0a_zpsb2797691.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385986i/745170._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 123b2f7e-cb78-4a11-bd8c-0e04d6479c0a_zpsb2797691.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>If you have read K.A’s Mystery Man, you know Tack. Kane ‘Tack’ Allen is a bad ass bossy biker. President of the MC Chaos. If you are like me, you fell for him in Mystery Man and wanted more. This is Tack’s story. <br/><br/>It all starts one night at the club. He meets a girl. Red.<br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/e96bd30a-d3bc-4dc0-a3d6-06079aa9c38f_zpsd1d7f6d6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385986i/745171.jpg' alt=' photo e96bd30a-d3bc-4dc0-a3d6-06079aa9c38f_zpsd1d7f6d6.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Red (aka Tyra) is not the typical girl Tack ‘sees’. He doesn’t know she is different at the time, but he finds out pretty quickly. After one night together, Tyra leaves Tack’s bed. What Tack</span>
  <span id="freeText4350900457782063057" style="display:none"><b>5 Hawt and Handsome Tack Stars </b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/123b2f7e-cb78-4a11-bd8c-0e04d6479c0a_zpsb2797691.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385986i/745170._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 123b2f7e-cb78-4a11-bd8c-0e04d6479c0a_zpsb2797691.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If you have read K.A’s Mystery Man, you know Tack. Kane ‘Tack’ Allen is a bad ass bossy biker. President of the MC Chaos. If you are like me, you fell for him in Mystery Man and wanted more. This is Tack’s story. <br><br>It all starts one night at the club. He meets a girl. Red.<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/e96bd30a-d3bc-4dc0-a3d6-06079aa9c38f_zpsd1d7f6d6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385986i/745171.jpg" alt=" photo e96bd30a-d3bc-4dc0-a3d6-06079aa9c38f_zpsd1d7f6d6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Red (aka Tyra) is not the typical girl Tack ‘sees’. He doesn’t know she is different at the time, but he finds out pretty quickly. After one night together, Tyra leaves Tack’s bed. What Tack doesn’t know is Tyra just got a new job working at the shop Tack owns. He tries to talk her into quitting, but she refuses. Tack doesn’t sleep with people he works with. She is persistent on staying and never sleeping with him again. <br><br> Tyra is thirty five years old, single- never been married. There is only one reason why. She is holding out for her Dream Man. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/waiting-on-my-prince-charming_zps896466b9.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385986i/745172.png" alt=" photo waiting-on-my-prince-charming_zps896466b9.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tack is not your typical Prince Charming. He has tattoos, rides a harley, has a crazy ass ex wife and two awesome kids. But Tyra just knows from the beginning he is it. She tries to fight it, but its no use. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“The perfect I was looking for wasn’t perfection. The perfect I was looking for was the one. And he was you.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>She knows Tack is the one for her because of one thing he does for her that no one else has been able to do. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/c4f6447c-b538-41a5-88c7-2f52833ddf55_zpse8c307e6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385986i/745173._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo c4f6447c-b538-41a5-88c7-2f52833ddf55_zpse8c307e6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I like everything about you, honey. Lived in black and white seems like all my life. Never noticed. Not until you colored my world.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> Tyra and Tack have a bumpy road. The more Tyra is around Tack, the more she starts to doubt their relationship. But after a while, Tack has his mind up about Tyra. And once he has made up his mind, there is no changing it. Tack sees the sweet side of Tyra, how good she is with his kids, how cute she is when she gets pissed at him. He starts to fall for her. Even though Tyra is trying to deny her feelings for Tack, its no use. <br><br>In the end- Tyra teaches Tack a few things...<br><b>
  <blockquote>Truth, honesty, perseverance, strength, love of all kinds and forgiveness are all beautiful, Tack. The most beautiful stories ever told are the most difficult to take.</blockquote>
</b><br>And Tack teaches Tyra a few things...<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/0f1f4f4b-bca8-4ec8-9597-57841fdf83ed_zpse37adb43.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385986i/745174.jpg" alt=" photo 0f1f4f4b-bca8-4ec8-9597-57841fdf83ed_zpse37adb43.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Babe, advice. A man expresses his gratitude, you do not throw attitude. You kiss him and, maybe, suck his dick to show your appreciation.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>They see the best in each other. I love it! <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Every day somethin' new. Will I ever get to the heart of you?”<br><br>“I’m not your absolution, honey. You earned it before you met me.”<br> “You’re my reward.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br>God this book was FANTASTIC! A little action, a little romance, a little funny, and A LOT of sexy= my kinda book! I love Tack even more then I did in Mystery Man. He is so great! Kristen Ashley writes the <b>best</b> alpha males. I loved Tack’s bossy attitude, tattoos, how he loved his kids, how incredibly sweet he could be and how freaking HOT he is! Oh yeah.. I liked Tyra too. There is nothing like a KA epilogue. This one was perfect. A book I will definitely be re-reading in the future! SO looking forward to Tabby and Shy’s book! <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/MMHarleys_zps60d6c5df.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385986i/745175.jpg" alt=" photo MMHarleys_zps60d6c5df.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_1409809405" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1409809405" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1409809405?book_show_action=true">Oct 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/21883167-motorcycle-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=mafia">mafia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=standalone">standalone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=crime">crime</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1409809405" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer951352300100479918"><b>5 **<u>colourful</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444385821i/16494745.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Life's a roller coaster. Best damn ride in the park. You don't close your eyes, hold on and wait for it to be over, babe. You keep your eyes open, lift your hands straight up in the air and enjoy the ride for as long as it lasts.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>All is right in the world again. After being more than a little disappointed by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515-law-man' rel='nofollow noopener'>Law Man</a> I was almost losing faith in Ms. Ashley for a second, but don’t fear my gently review readers, she hit it out of the park with this one. Uber sexy b</span>
  <span id="freeText951352300100479918" style="display:none"><b>5 **<u>colourful</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444385821i/16494745.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Life's a roller coaster. Best damn ride in the park. You don't close your eyes, hold on and wait for it to be over, babe. You keep your eyes open, lift your hands straight up in the air and enjoy the ride for as long as it lasts.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>All is right in the world again. After being more than a little disappointed by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515-law-man" rel="nofollow noopener">Law Man</a> I was almost losing faith in Ms. Ashley for a second, but don’t fear my gently review readers, she hit it out of the park with this one. Uber sexy biker bad boy, feisty heroine, excellent chemistry, a little action and major swoon fest. I’m yet again in my KA wonderland bubble. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13448656-motorcycle-man" rel="nofollow noopener">Motorcycle Man</a> is the fourth and last instalment in the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/69395-dream-man" rel="nofollow noopener">Dream Man series</a> and at last we get to enjoy Tack's story. Over the course of the series we have seen a lot of the notorious Chaos MC president. We first met him as the mysterious and smoking hot biker who had a little standoff with Hawk and Lawson regarding Gwen’s heart...and we all know who won that fight. *sigh*Hawk*sigh* But I digress, he slowly but surely became a household name in the subsequent books, helping out in precarious situations and having his hands in all kinds of dangerous dealings. To say I was curious to see where his story would lead was the understatement of the century. Especially since everyone told me his was the book to read. Well, I can second that. Fan-freaking-tastic ride.<br><br>Let's talk story.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I’m Chaos?”<br>“Was my dick just in you?”<br>I fought an annoyed growl and said, “Uh... yeah.”<br>“Then you’re Chaos.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Tack and Tyra’s story starts with a bang. Pun intended. Yes, you should take that literally. Tyra attends one of the Chaos MC’s parties and the moment she lays eyes on Tack she is a gonner. Over tequila and roast pork sandwiches she falls in love and eventually into bed with him. One hot hook-up and in the end he tells her to leave. Slam, bam, thank you ma’am.<br><br>That’s where the real problem starts. She is not only crushed by his less than cavalier behaviour (biker, anyone?) but there is also the minor issue of her being the garage’s new office manager. Yup, fucking the boss always ends well.<br><br>What can I say? I freaking love this set-up. It might sound instalove-ish, but don’t worry his actions have quite the opposite effect on Tyra. But regardless she needs the job and when they meet again the next day she fights for it too. What ensues is a delicious battle of wills. Tack is used to getting respect and talkback is not usual for him, but the moment the sassy redhead gets in his face he starts to get a little more interested in the woman - in addition to wanting her naked on the office desk.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1444387714i/16494969.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I absolutely adored Tyra. She doesn’t cave in and bends herself to fit into Tack’s world without getting something from him in return. She is not accustomed to the MC life. For all intents and purposes two worlds are clashing together here. She wears fancy pencil skirts and high heels and he is a rough biker, but they sure know how to make it work. I actually think when it comes to the <i>Dream Man</i> heroines Tyra wins the competition by a mile. She is feisty, outspoken, can handle herself and knows what she wants. Or she knew it until she met a kick-ass biker and learned the hard way that life can be colourful and being a biker babe is pretty darn cool, drama notwithstanding.<br><br>Drama being a crazy ex-wife, the russian mob, teenagers in the house and McGyvering with Aunt Bette. The latter quite possibly qualifying as one of my favourite things in the whole damn book. I need me an Aunt like that.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“The most beautiful stories ever told are the most difficult to take.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>What can I say about Tack? Well, you have to meet him. He actually manages to stand out in a long line of alpha- male-dream-men. Not an easy task. He is a bit stoic, a whole lot in control, naughty and more than a little secretive. Naturally he has a heart of gold and once you peel back the layers and get to the history, what brought him here, he becomes one of those unforgettable book boyfriends.<br><br>I'm both a KA fan and a lover of MC books, but up until now I wasn't sure if the two together would make such a good combination. Well, now I know they do. It's a sweet balance between a swoon worthy love story with a little edge, courtesy of the dangers MC life brings to the table. Tack being the president of said club and living in an outlaw world reacts a little different to relationship matters. And it's fun. On top of that it makes for good stories and Ms. Ashley’s highly descriptive and very detailed style felt a little less strained as well.<br><br>Lastly, I’m thrilled to read more about the Chaos boys in their own little book series. Yes, I’m most definitely addicted. ;P<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1441631277i/16131398.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="951352300100479918" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1538647926" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9016922873959167897">Find all of my reviews at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/'>http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br/><br/>If you follow me, you’ll know I put out a “gimmegimme” for a motorcycle book recommendation after watching the new television series <i>Outsiders</i>. Basically, I wanted to drink wine out of a box and read a book starring this guy . . . . <br/><br/><a href='http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454946522ra/18033200.gif' alt='Palm Springs commercial photography' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>#boooiiiiiiiinnnnnnnngggggggg<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4702933-mrsjoseph' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mrs. Joseph</a> was the first to reply and boy did she provide a good one. The basics of the story are as follows: Tyra quit her old job and has been in hot pursuit of a new one</span>
  <span id="freeText9016922873959167897" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br>If you follow me, you’ll know I put out a “gimmegimme” for a motorcycle book recommendation after watching the new television series <i>Outsiders</i>. Basically, I wanted to drink wine out of a box and read a book starring this guy . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454946522ra/18033200.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>#boooiiiiiiiinnnnnnnngggggggg<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4702933-mrsjoseph" rel="nofollow noopener">Mrs. Joseph</a> was the first to reply and boy did she provide a good one. The basics of the story are as follows: Tyra quit her old job and has been in hot pursuit of a new one. She also decided she needed to let a little of her inner freak out and bangs a motorcycle dude the night before she starts her new gig. When she shows up for her first day on the job things don’t go quite as planned when she is greeted by new boss, Tack . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“I do not work with bitches who’ve had my dick in their mouth.”</i>
</b><br><br>Offended by him yet? Good. Get the eff outta here ‘cause he’s mine anyway. Tack is all of the following . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“Coarse, vulgar, uncouth . . . rude.”</i>
</b><br><br>And I was singing “YAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAY!” because that’s exactly what I was hoping for. As I said in my plea for porn, to quote the late and great Aaliyah “sometimes I’m goody goody, but right now I’m naughty naughty” . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454946522ra/18033201.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I was looking for a leading male who was exactly the way Tack described himself . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“I ain’t no choir boy.”</i>
</b><br><br>Nope, but he sho ‘nuff made me say Hallelujah a time or twelve. Holy hizzle . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454946522ra/18033202.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I started this book not giving <b>any</b> shits if Tack was a chauvinist or womanizer or criminal or whatever else could be awful. I don’t get offended easily and I sure as hell wasn’t going to allow myself to get offended by a character who very easily could have been written as offensive on purpose. Imagine my delight when I found out not only was the Chaos motorcycle club different from the stereotype . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“We don’t transport drugs. We don’t offer enforcement. We don’t sell tail. We don’t sell guns. We build cars and sell auto supplies.”</i>
</b><br><br>But Tack was different than the stereotype as well . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“You take my hand again like you did that night, I’ll guide you through the nightmare. We’ll make it to the other side and I promise, along the way, you’ll enjoy the ride.”</i>
</b><br><br>This was one hell of a ride. Kristen Ashley, you are my official hotline bling . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454946522ra/18033203.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’m withholding the final star because <i>Motorcycle Man</i> did get a weeeeee bit long in the tooth when it came to the make up/break up B.S. (seriously, just STFU and bang him ya dumbass ‘cause he’s smokin’ hot) and because I have high hopes that things will just keep getting better (I’ve already got the first in the Chaos series cued up and ready to go). Now who’s ready for some of my sloppy seconds with Tack????<br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454946522ra/18033204.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>ORIGINAL "REVIEW":</b><br><br>Mrs. Joseph assures me this mechanical journal will teach me all about the complexities of the modern internal combustion engine . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/california/palm-springs/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454708099ra/18003590.gif" alt="Palm Springs commercial photography" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Zoom zoom.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12544240959416923688"><b>★Book Basics★ </b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Genre</i>
</b>: - Cont Romance<br/><b>
  <i>Series</i>
</b>: - 4th in the series<br/><b>
  <i>Love triangle?</i>
</b> - <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[No <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><b>
  <i>Cheating?</i>
</b> - <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[No, although <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ the hero does have a ONS with another woman (off page) after he has a ONS with the heroine, but before there is any hint of a relationship with the heroine <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><b>
  <i>HEA? -</i>
</b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[Yes <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><b>
  <i>Would I read more by this author/or in this series? </i>
</b>- Yes<br/><b>
  <i>Rating </i>
</b>- 5 ++++<br/><br/><br/><b>★Rev</b></span>
  <span id="freeText12544240959416923688" style="display:none"><b>★Book Basics★ </b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Genre</i>
</b>: - Cont Romance<br /><b>
  <i>Series</i>
</b>: - 4th in the series<br /><b>
  <i>Love triangle?</i>
</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>
  <i>Cheating?</i>
</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No, although <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ the hero does have a ONS with another woman (off page) after he has a ONS with the heroine, but before there is any hint of a relationship with the heroine <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>
  <i>HEA? -</i>
</b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><b>
  <i>Would I read more by this author/or in this series? </i>
</b>- Yes<br /><b>
  <i>Rating </i>
</b>- 5 ++++<br /><br /><br /><b>★Review★</b><br /><br />So, this must be my 5th/6th re read of this book, and I still love it.<br /><br />It may not be for everyone, Tack is after all the biker boss to end all biker bosses, rude, bossy, swears a lot, has a short fuse, drinks tequila like it is water, and eats more pork than one man should. But he is a man, who loves life and enjoys it.<br /><br />Tyra, is careful, has a take out night, does yoga, drinks green tea, but is still kick-ass and feisty.<br /><br />They have a bumpy start, but once Tack realises who Tyra is as a person, he is determined to have her, and make her live her life. He may be all the things we see at the start of the book, but as it goes on, and we get to know his past, and how he is as he is, you can understand how he is so much more. He is so loving and it is obvious how much Tyra means to him and how much he wants her to mean to him.<br /><br />Love love love, probably my favourite of this series. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"You don't know this, baby, but some men have dream women too"</b>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/355171063?book_show_action=true">Jun 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=super-cheese">super-cheese</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer355171063" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11863513223044516362"><b>If you liked this book and you aren't watching the show Sons of Anarchy, I'm going to have to ask you why the *censored* not?</b><br/><br/>For reals. Tack could be in SoA. Half of this story could be on the show SoA. Yes, I said for reals. Deal with it. SoA is a kickass show, btw. It's on Netflix streaming and DvD. If you have Netflix, go check it out. I will give you a pass only if you're not Stateside.<br/><br/>Boo. It's killing me to have to go and write another 3 star review. You do not know how BADLY I wanted to g</span>
  <span id="freeText11863513223044516362" style="display:none"><b>If you liked this book and you aren't watching the show Sons of Anarchy, I'm going to have to ask you why the *censored* not?</b><br /><br />For reals. Tack could be in SoA. Half of this story could be on the show SoA. Yes, I said for reals. Deal with it. SoA is a kickass show, btw. It's on Netflix streaming and DvD. If you have Netflix, go check it out. I will give you a pass only if you're not Stateside.<br /><br />Boo. It's killing me to have to go and write another 3 star review. You do not know how BADLY I wanted to go up to 4 stars. The first 25% of the book was so much fun! And then the middle of the book happened. I put this book down to go read something else, came back and read a few pages, put it down to go read something else, etc. I was working on finishing up today and found my mind wandering and put the reader aside for a few to go clean and when I came back, I realized that I had <b>put the reader away in the <i>middle</i> of a sex scene.</b> This has to be the first time that's ever happened.<br /><br /><b>I hate not loving books that several of my friends love.</b> You don't know how badly this sucks for me. It's WAY more fun to love a book and have friends to get excited about it with. Being the loner kid at the party is NOT fun. Granted, I do have friends who are absolutely not fans of KA but we're not going to go make a fun group to talk about how we don't love the books. So yeah...it sucks being on the outskirts when a bunch of friends love something and you don't. *sigh*<br /><br />It isn't that I find this author's books to be bad because they're not. They're just long for no real reason - too much content is either filler or is a repeat of itself (this book had 3 different times where the girl tried to break off the fledgling relationship and that's not counting the times she tried to quit her job to get away from him). If these books could be cut back and rearranged, I think we'd have a lot more to work with. Tack was sexy. Tack's dirty talk was sexy. Tack's protective nature was sexy. Tack's story about the hand around the throat (if you don't know, don't ask) was completely and totally endearing.<br /><br />I made the point in my review of <i>Mystery Man</i> that all of the KA book heroes seem to sound the same, so I won't go into detail of that again, but it's still an issue. Men simply do not all sound like clones, especially when they come from different cultures, cities and ways-of-life. When you have a pimp, a mountain man, a commando, and a motorcycle club leader all sounding alike, this shows a huge weak spot in character creation and development.<br /><br />We had yet another kidnapping in this book. I could possibly see this in different series but recycled plots in the same series? <br /><br />We had another guy liking another girl for the same exact reason. <i>"You give it good, darlin', that attitude."</i><br /><br />I just can't get excited about books where the best part of it is that the "guy is sexy." There are tons of great books with more to offer which still have sexy men and steamy hot scenes. There needs to be more that I'm getting from my stories aside from excess filler, repeated plot devices and recycled character qualities. <br /><br /><b>So does this make me a hater?</b><br /><br />No. Absolutely not. 3 stars is NEVER a "dislike" review from me. It's usually my "okay," "average," or "liked but wasn't impressed" rating. I loved the beginning of the book. I loved the end of the book. This also seems to be a repeating feeling of mine. <i>Parts</i> of each KA book are truly enjoyable. Unfortunately, there is way too much extra stuff that simply isn't worth my time. I don't want to know about Uncle whoever and the fourth and fifth co-worker and the random people the characters know from another book series who showed up at the hospital. <br /><br /><b>Am I officially throwing in the towel?</b><br /><br />Who knows. As of right now, I'm taking a break. I think I'll try to finish out the Colorado Mountain series at some point and maybe try the standalone that was recommended to me. I can't say that I'm going to be in any hurry to do so, however. <br /><br /><b>Best quote of the book :</b><br /><br /><i>"Enjoying the fuck out of the show. Shit, Cherry, you're cute, all badass and pissed off and kickin' squirrel-ball ass."</i><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11863513223044516362" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer4087234636675233258"><b> 4 Stars<i> (Originally Read 2/21/2014)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 3.5 Stars<i> (Re-Read 3/22/2017)</i></b><br/><br/><b>3.5 Stars<i> (*Re-Read 10/14/2019)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This was a re-read that I've been putting off for some reason. I think I knew I probably wouldn't like it as much as I did, and sadly that is true. I'm going to drop my rating from 4 stars to 3.5. I couldn't get over how my mental impression of Tack was so far off! I really enjoyed him the first time, and I held him on my KA hero pedestal for a long time. Sadly, I just found him to b</span>
  <span id="freeText4087234636675233258" style="display:none"><b> 4 Stars<i> (Originally Read 2/21/2014)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 3.5 Stars<i> (Re-Read 3/22/2017)</i></b><br /><br /><b>3.5 Stars<i> (*Re-Read 10/14/2019)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This was a re-read that I've been putting off for some reason. I think I knew I probably wouldn't like it as much as I did, and sadly that is true. I'm going to drop my rating from 4 stars to 3.5. I couldn't get over how my mental impression of Tack was so far off! I really enjoyed him the first time, and I held him on my KA hero pedestal for a long time. Sadly, I just found him to be an OTT pushy jerk for most of the book! I still enjoyed it, and I still will keep this as one of my favorite KA books...but I'm a little disappointed :(<br /><br /><b>*Re-Read Update</b>- I'm keeping my rating the same. I skimmed a good bit, but mostly because I knew what was going to happen. Still don't love Tack as much as I initially did, but still did like him some...<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Tyra and Tack's story. Tyra made some big life changes and gets a job as an office manager for a garage. She puts on her brace face on her first day because she was kicked out her new bosses bed the day before after she thought she had finally met her dream man. Tack isn't happy to find out that his ONS is also his new office manager, and he lets her know it in a not-so-nice way. They dance around each other some, but Tack soon realizes that Tyra is what he's been looking for and goes full pursuit. There is friend and family drama, some typical mc drama, and some sexy times...and they do get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This was told in Tyra's POV (with some small sections in other character's POVs).<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. It's a typical KA longer read, but I never skimmed and I thought it flowed well.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Kind of, but not the type that irritates me.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 3 stars. Tack. I went into this with Tack as my #2 KA hero, but he was a major jerk through most of it! He definitely dropped the ranks after this re-read :(<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 3.5 stars. Tyra. I liked her, but I wanted her to be stronger in expressing her feelings at times.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Moderate. I shed a few tears, but I never needed any tissues.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They both push and pull at times. The H was the main pursuer of the relationship.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Good. They have some good tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>Safe sex:</b> No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I don't remember any mention of condoms, birth control, std statuses, or previous practices. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The H was seen after he first hooked up with the h (the next day) kissing OW and walking her out to her car in the morning after an implied night together. This OW causes some drama for the h and H later on.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Scene with h seeing side character cheating on his old lady <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[They are separated shortly (days?), but there was no mention or suggestion of other partners during this time.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Violence/murder, kidnapping, drug use/dealing, and the H had an ex wife and two children from previous marriage.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had good closure with a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>How I got it:</b> I bought it for $3.99 on Amazon back in 2014.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe with exception</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does</b> have the h and H pushing away at times<br />- <b> Does</b> have a short (days?) separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does </b> have abuse (not by mcs)<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have OTT sad parts<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_619911079" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/619911079" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/619911079?book_show_action=true">May 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">KA Fans, Biker genre</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer619911079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3646481942026612750"><b>5 Claimed and Accepted Stars <br/>* ** * * <i>Spoiler Free- Many Re-read Reviews :D</i><br/>This character Tack leaped off the pages from the first <i>Dream Man book, Mystery Man</i>. From the minute he was introduced, he commanded attention. I think KA thought about him and with the way she presented him throughout the entire series, she was priming us for the Chaos books. The timing was right, <i>Sons of Anarchy</i> had become a hit and she was there on the pulse of knowing what readers wanted. <br/><br/>She made him a man who would </b></span>
  <span id="freeText3646481942026612750" style="display:none"><b>5 Claimed and Accepted Stars <br>* ** * * <i>Spoiler Free- Many Re-read Reviews :D</i><br>This character Tack leaped off the pages from the first <i>Dream Man book, Mystery Man</i>. From the minute he was introduced, he commanded attention. I think KA thought about him and with the way she presented him throughout the entire series, she was priming us for the Chaos books. The timing was right, <i>Sons of Anarchy</i> had become a hit and she was there on the pulse of knowing what readers wanted. <br><br>She made him a man who would seem at first very straight forward... almost a caricature when introduced...but by the time we finished Mystery Man, we knew there was much more to Tack. <br><br>In this book, we finally got it all.<br><br>The woman he focuses on is Tyra. I had difficulties with her because I never really got her. Oh, I ended up understanding her...but her thought process was sometimes annoying to me. <br><br>She came from a very set family. Her parents loved Ohio, had a set way of living; could be judgmental but loved her completely. She had a vision in her head of only setting her cap for her Dream Man...She had had only 5 men in her life and made the error of thinking they could be molded or fixed... but it just didn't click. She had a position in a non-dis-script company- we never really know what she did before working at Ride... where she became the supervisor and was targeted by a co worker who made her life miserable. She made enough to purchase a house and have it fixed up to her liking. She was living her life but decided to shake it up...make changes. <br><br>I get all of the above...but still throughout the book, there were moments she didn't make sense...her mouth said one thing but then her actions did another....and to be an equal opportunity player... Tack had his moments too...which were jaw-dropping... over the top claiming.<br><br>But in the end... you either buy into whatever KA is presenting or you don't. It is as easy as that... and with the idea of Chaos, Tack and his quick, true love Tyra, once you were in... you were set for a safe, strong ride. I will say this club was not the Heavy Biker Scene like the <b>Susan Fanetti series Signal Bend</b>, which I love. This was a club that had had its dark... and was moved to the light by Tack over the years... Oh, they are still bikers for sure... but we are not there when they may have wreaked their presence and littered bodies in their wake. <br><br>The coming together of these also touches on Tack's past attraction to Hawk's Gwen. It is important because she was a woman who he felt more for ....wanted to see if it was it for him... and lost out to Hawk. What is interesting is he still has her a friend and it does come into play here... not sexually but supportive. It also reflects that Tack was open to having a real relationship... more than hook ups. We see his love for his children; his intrigue for Tyra and all of it comes together where we want more than the Delicious Epilogue.... we are primed and ready for the next series Chaos. <br><br>My review below was from the 2nd read of this book with the C.D.Canaries. I think it still remains true.</b><br><br> <i>This was a re-read, thanks to the wonderful C D Canaries! 2/2014</i><br><br>I first discovered KA over a year ago. I cannot remember if this or At Peace was my first book. I can say this was my first biker experience outside of watching Sons of Anarchy (which I loved).<br><br>It took me a moment to learn how to read KA, to figure out the flow and logic to her phrasing and concepts. I wasn't at first sure what was going on but once I got it... I.GOT.IT.<br><br>I am not going to go into the particulars of this story... I just am going to say...until you accept the biker code, Tack could seem over the top in his concept of... I have claimed you... therefore you can't go... but once you do accept this code... then his character and everything he stands for... is golden. <br><br>Do these KA men exist in the real world... I don't know. I do know, if we are lucky, we get bits and pieces along the way and it is our job to know when the "sweet" is being given.<br><br>On a side note.... after reading this book and At Peace, I proceeded to read every single KA book I could get my hands on outside of her fantasy series. Yup, I read 23 books in a row and was not sorry one little bit. (the Fantasy series is up next for me)<br><br>Re-reading these books can bring about a fresh mind ... and when you read as much as we all do, I highly advise you to find that happy place anytime you need to... I know I just did.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_" title="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1483487036l/12299419._SX50_.jpg" alt="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1)<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/651399020">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12881141.Wild_Man__Dream_Man___2_" title="Wild Man (Dream Man, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener"><img <div id="review_761536682" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/761536682" />
    <a title="Deborah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24383684-deborah"><img alt="Deborah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515068567p2/24383684.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/761536682?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Deborah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Deborah" href="/user/show/24383684-deborah">Deborah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24383684-deborah?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer761536682" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17449273554543266362">This is one of my go to books, I've lost count of how many times I've actually read this. When I really started to get into reading again (after a break when my children were young and I just didn't get time to read) Kristen Ashley was my favourite author her books were just so much more than anything I'd previously come across. The problem is I can't remember the last time I wasn't disappointed in one of her books to the extent where I've given up on her new stuff completely, but enough moaning</span>
  <span id="freeText17449273554543266362" style="display:none">This is one of my go to books, I've lost count of how many times I've actually read this. When I really started to get into reading again (after a break when my children were young and I just didn't get time to read) Kristen Ashley was my favourite author her books were just so much more than anything I'd previously come across. The problem is I can't remember the last time I wasn't disappointed in one of her books to the extent where I've given up on her new stuff completely, but enough moaning back to the book.<br />This is a fabulous book with some great characters Tack being one of my favourite all time alpha males.<br />Tyra has made some life changes, she's left her job and started afresh which is why she finds herself at Ride, The Chaos MC and the man of her dreams. She's spent her adult life looking for her dream man and she'll settle for nothing less it's one promise she made to herself a long long time ago and now she's found him, Kane "Tack" Allen. Their eyes meet over a sea of people, they drink tequila and head to his room and it's all good. It's better than good, it's perfect. Tyra is basking in the glow of knowing she's found her man and her future, until he opens his mouth.<br />“Babe, you awake?”......<br />“I’m awake,”.....<br />“Time to get to your own bed, darlin’.”.....<br />“Leave your number and close the door on your way out, would you, Red?”<br />To say Tack's not happy when he discovers Tyra's his new office manager is an understatement, he fires her on the spot but Tyra needs the job and Tack learns there's a whole lot more to the woman in front of him than he originally thought.<br />I've read 3 of the 4 books in this series (not really sure why but Brock's book never really appealed to me) and the characters we loved from them are back along with a whole host of sexy bikers and a story that keeps you reading, along with lots of hot sex. Who could ask for more?<br />###<br />Just done another re-read and while I still love Tack just as much as I ever did Tyra annoyed me more this time. I nearly had whiplash with the number of times she was leaving, yes she was definitely going this time...okay well next time it's a definite....maybe.<br />I don't know why she annoyed me this time but it's still a fabulous book </span>
  <a data-text-id="17449273554543266362" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/280351324" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=biker-hero">biker-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=alpha-hero">alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer280351324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4686220566662299345">Oh, yes. This is Vintage Ashley.<br/><br/>I loved every freaking second of it. It was just perfect. Been waiting a while for Tack's story since he first growled onto the page in Mystery Man and it's definitely been worth the wait.<br/><br/>He's everything an Ashley Alpha should be - he's arrogant, rude, domineering, bossy and impossibly HOT! I was appalled with the way he behaved to Tyra after their first night together but I knew he would redeem himself.<br/><br/>What I love about a Kristen Ashley hero is that they may be c</span>
  <span id="freeText4686220566662299345" style="display:none">Oh, yes. This is Vintage Ashley.<br /><br />I loved every freaking second of it. It was just perfect. Been waiting a while for Tack's story since he first growled onto the page in Mystery Man and it's definitely been worth the wait.<br /><br />He's everything an Ashley Alpha should be - he's arrogant, rude, domineering, bossy and impossibly HOT! I was appalled with the way he behaved to Tyra after their first night together but I knew he would redeem himself.<br /><br />What I love about a Kristen Ashley hero is that they may be complete dickheads but, somehow, they know when they fall in love, when they have something special, they claim that woman and they go all out to let the world know that she is their's and to protect her. It gives me the warm and fuzzies. I don't care how un-PC that is, I just love it.<br /><br />Tyra is a great heroine - she's honest, sweet, vulnerable yet also tough as nails and nothing will hold her back from protecting and defending the people she cares about. Tack is more of the same and then some. <br /><br />I also loved the whole badass biker MC vibe, the Brotherhood - I'm so glad that there's going to be a new series revolving around Chaos. Bring it on. I loved their tattoos and their sweet touching moments. It was all good.<br /><br />BUT - KA you have raised the bar exponentially here. Tack is going to be a <i>very</i> hard act to follow.<br /><br />I f*cking loved this. It's the dogs bollocks.<br /><br />5 big and shiny stars contemporary romance<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="4686220566662299345" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_271767203" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
