    <a title="Searock" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6641663-searock"><img alt="Searock" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396402019p2/6641663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/271767203?book_show_action=true">Feb 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Searock" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Searock" href="/user/show/6641663-searock">Searock</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6641663-searock?shelf=my-world-revolves-around-the-ka-sun">my-world-revolves-around-the-ka-sun</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer271767203" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11086690177460482217"><br/>I am wrung out and sated.<br/>Wow.<br/>What a fantastic book! <br/>It's a fabulous conclusion to the <i>best series ever, ever, ever (not a pnr fan so, no, "those" series' don't count), ever, ever, ever</i>!<br/>This book just got deeper and deeper, better and better. <br/><br/>I had read the teaser chapters on the author's blog ages ago, so I felt like it took a while for me to get back into the story. It also felt like Tack and Tyra were arguing a lot, which I normally like, but this started to resemble siblings in the backseat o</span>
  <span id="freeText11086690177460482217" style="display:none"><br>I am wrung out and sated.<br>Wow.<br>What a fantastic book! <br>It's a fabulous conclusion to the <i>best series ever, ever, ever (not a pnr fan so, no, "those" series' don't count), ever, ever, ever</i>!<br>This book just got deeper and deeper, better and better. <br><br>I had read the teaser chapters on the author's blog ages ago, so I felt like it took a while for me to get back into the story. It also felt like Tack and Tyra were arguing a lot, which I normally like, but this started to resemble siblings in the backseat of a car: <br>Yes you did. <br>No I didn't.<br>Yes, you did.<br>No, I didn't.<br>(not actual dialog, btw, but you get the idea)<br><br>I was also annoyed with Tack early on bc he was being too pushy (literally) for a half a minute, his hands were always at Tyra's throat and he often held her and wouldn't let her go even when she asked him to. Then (then!) something fabulous happens and KA (author-goddess extraordinaire) brought it around, worked it all together for good, hit her stride and rocked my world. <br>(and rocked it and rocked it and kept rockin' it til the climax, which was amazing!) <br>Whee! <br>I would say I'm jk, but it really did work out like that :)<br><br>Let me just tell you, my issue with Tack holding on to Tyra especially with his hands on her throat metamorphosed into a <b>thing of beauty</b> (you'll see!) and the constant bickering became witty, fun banter. Those are just two of dozens of great elements in this book. Some of these are signature KA details (huge cast, a background drama that drives action, ex-spouses, etc), others seem added to bring closure to the series as well as introduce a new series, and some are the little behind-the-scenes gears and mechanisms that always effortlessly whir along with simple complexity in most every KA read. These are so organic, so straight out of her heart and mind, that its practically unnoticeable, but they make for a richer experience. <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[It's stuff like the "roller-coaster" thing, <i>The Color Purple</i>, the "pulse" thing, giving her "sweet", counting the "honeys", the "colors" thing, he let me go/not letting go/she let me go. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>*sigh*<br>Don't mind me, I am a fan.<br><br>A warning for those who have trouble reading the KA dialog that sounds like, <br>Um, <br>Eh... um, <br>Tack, <br>Red, <br>Um... <br>Tyra, <br>Tack", etc.<br>There is a lot of mumbling and interruption that shows up in the dialog here too. If that's gonna kill it for you, I can't recommend you read this book. I think you would miss out on a <b>great read</b>, but it's fair warning. <br><br>For me, I have become fluent in KA alpha-speak and heroine-mumble by way of immersion. I can breeze through that dialog because to me, it's a brand or a style. I am going on a journey to a place that has a pidgin language that one needs to learn to engage in trade or something (Ha!). In my mind it's part of the KA experience and does not take away from but actually adds to great characterization. <br><br>Note: I re-read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_" title="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/books/1327912964s/12299419.jpg" alt="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_" title="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Mystery Man</a> just prior to this release and it made the experience even better for me. I rec if it's been awhile since you started this series to reacquaint yourself with Tack in that book first. <br><br>I also read the blog post KA put up about missing Tack and it gave me awesome closure. <br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.kristenashley.net/menu/blog.html">http://www.kristenashley.net/menu/blo...</a><br>*big, gorgeous sigh*<br>*basking*<br>*smiling*<br>*thinking about (Watch Out!! Spoilers!) girl posses and next-generation babies and "blood brothers" and Shy and Tabby and badasses from different walks who have each other's backs and riding the Rocky's to Napa and the California Coast and a hundred other Kit-cracky, KAwesome cool things*<br><br>The books I love are the hardest to write about. I expect I'll have a real review ready by this time next year.<br><br><b>Sh*t I googled while reading</b>:<br>*Harley Davidson Dyna Glide<br>*badass biker goatee images<br>*Mustang Eleanor Fastback<br>*Storage Wars: Brandi<br>*Saw (What? I don't watch scary stuff)<br>*Dragon tattoo images<br><br><b>For the fans</b>:<br>Lots of stuff in here.<br>(don't peek unless you've read it!)<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>"Greedy."<br><br>Tack wrapping his fingers around Tyra's neck.<br>"... he let her pulse beat into his fingers and he did it until it washed the memories away."<br>and... super spoiler <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[around his newborn son's <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Love the way Tyra had a tough time with "sweet", telling Hop not to be sweet with her and treat her like the badass she is, lol!<br><br>Tack sounding all hardcore telling Tyra that when she turns off Broadway into Ride, she's in his world, but watching his transformation into a major sweetheart was gorgeous.<br><br>Can I get a "what, what(?)" for how deftly KA weaves issues of drug use, infidelity, illegal behavior and other hot potato issues with the lightest touch. This was the supporting cast taking part in this and, as a reader, I didn't even flinch. It's masterful.<br><br>“Because you’re gonna live life, Red. I’m gonna teach you to suck it dry.”<br><br>"Chattin’ with bikers like they were insurance brokers".<br><br>"Love and redemption. You said, ‘the most beautiful stories ever told are the most difficult to take’. You said that, Red. Right out. And I knew if you got that, when it was later and I shared my shit with you, you’d get me."<br><br>“She’s dark, you’re red. I’ll fuck dark, I’ll fuck sun but only red has staying power. Considered sun once. Lost her. Now it’s you.”<br>(What a romantic, right? Gah! Not.)<br><br>“So what’s with the sass?” <br>“It’s me.” <br>“It is,” he sighed. “Fuck me.” <br>“You said you like it,” I reminded him. <br><br>“Wild and sweet, can both snarl like a bitch or purr like a kitten.”<br><br>“Babe, look at me.” <br>“Kiss my ass,” I replied.<br>(LOL)<br><br>"I needed him to go out and get his own sandwich so I could get in my own car and drive to Vancouver."<br><br>“I don’t have kitchen utensils from Mars, babe."<br><br>I loved the verbal smackdown that Tyra gives Tack at about 35%. It is an eloquent combination punch. I loved it almost as much or equal to Dusty's. My heart was in my throat and my mind was chanting, "you go, Red"!<br><br>(this one hurt)<br>"You have to be you and you can’t be you around me without me getting chewed up in the process..."<br><br>Gah, the rollercoaster metaphor was so good in here. The way it was so true for Tyra to feel she needed to get off it and how Tack transformed it to raising your hands and enjoying the ride.<br><br>"Now, you’re gonna kiss me so I can get back to work, you can go home and come to a foregone conclusion.”<br><br>His lips curved and he asked, “Woo you?” <br>“Woo me!” I snapped.<br><br>“Fuck me, now she’s bein’ sweet.” <br>I laughed softly and offered, “You want me to get pissed and maybe throw a rant?” <br>“No, ‘cause that makes me hard too.”<br><br>“Three.” <br>“Pardon?” <br>“Three honeys.” <br>He was counting. “Now you’re being sweet,” I whispered. <br>“You gonna fall apart on me?” <br>“I’ll try not to.”<br><br>It's on every page peeps!!!! <br>How many characters do I have left for this review? <br>*checks the bottom of the edit window*<br><br>“And you forget tonight, I’ll be pissed.” <br>“I won’t forget, Tack.” <br>“Be sure about that.” <br>“I won’t forget.”<br><br>“I hit the heart of you yet?” Tack asked. <br>“Close,” I whispered. <br>“Tastes sweet,” he whispered back and I felt my eyes get wet. <br>“Yeah,” I agreed quietly, “it does.”<br><br>“Another layer, I lay my shit out, all of it, it’s ugly and she ends that by bein’ cute.” <br>“Shut up.” <br>“And bossy.” <br>“Shut up.” <br>“Bossy and a cry baby.” <br>“Shut up!”<br><br>“Uh… you pledged your troth to me, Tack. It’s not like you don’t know I get feisty.” <br>“I pledged my troth,” Tack repeated. <br>“Yeah.” <br>“You just said I pledged my troth.” <br>“Yes, that’s what I just said.” <br>“What’s a troth?” <br>“I don’t know, I just know you pledged it.”<br><br><br>“Don’t let me go,” she whispered. <br>“I won’t let you go, Red.” <br>“Don’t let me go.” <br>“I won’t let you go, baby.” <br>“Don’t let me go.”<br><br>"She let him go."<br><br>(Gah, there was a lot of letting go and not letting go up in here!!)<br><br>"<i>You</i> are my absolution.”<br><br>Alternating heroine POVs for the win!!<br><br>“Go to him, Sweet Pea,”<br>(Oh gah... Hawk)<br><br>“... brace, baby, ‘cause I’m about to get sweet and you need to process it fast so you can move on to suckin’ me off, <i>not fast</i>.”<br>(LOL! The stuff Tack says after that trumps all the sweet he ever gave her.)<br><br>Happy epilogue joy. She managed to pull in the whole universe for that. Woot!<br><br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Michele ~ la Smoocherina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina"><img alt="Michele ~ la Smoocherina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1418082097p2/5897822.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/290664023?book_show_action=true">Mar 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michele ~ la Smoocherina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michele ~ la Smoocherina" href="/user/show/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina">Michele ~ la Smoocherina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=emotionally-satisfying">emotionally-satisfying</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=hot-as-hell">hot-as-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=features-a-good-father">features-a-good-father</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=good-dirty-talk-or-phone-sex">good-dirty-talk-or-phone-sex</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=character-biker">character-biker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5897822-michele-la-smoocherina?shelf=strong-heroine">strong-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer290664023" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10586863153051188341">As reviewed for <a href='http://readourlipsblog.blogspot.com/2012/05/review-motorcycle-man-by-kristen-ashley.html#more' rel='nofollow noopener'>Read Our Lips Book Blog!</a><br/><br/>Tack! We finally get Tack’s book and boy was he worth the wait! We first met Tack in Mystery Man, Book one of the Dream Man Series. Click here for that review. He’s a hot biker guy, who’s a real badass in the ‘protect and take care of what’s mine’ arena of the Alpha Male, and Kristen Ashley can write the hell out of an Alpha Male!<br/><br/>Tyra is a smart, got-it-all-together chick, who has been living off of her savings for the past two months after leaving a toxic</span>
  <span id="freeText10586863153051188341" style="display:none">As reviewed for <a href="http://readourlipsblog.blogspot.com/2012/05/review-motorcycle-man-by-kristen-ashley.html#more" rel="nofollow noopener">Read Our Lips Book Blog!</a><br><br>Tack! We finally get Tack’s book and boy was he worth the wait! We first met Tack in Mystery Man, Book one of the Dream Man Series. Click here for that review. He’s a hot biker guy, who’s a real badass in the ‘protect and take care of what’s mine’ arena of the Alpha Male, and Kristen Ashley can write the hell out of an Alpha Male!<br><br>Tyra is a smart, got-it-all-together chick, who has been living off of her savings for the past two months after leaving a toxic work environment. We meet Tyra after she’s had a one night stand with Tack, thinking he’s her dream man, but after some seriously hot sex, he kicks her out of bed and it breaks her heart a little. Fast forward a day or two we get to see Tyra show up for her first day of work at Ride, the garage belonging to Chaos, the Biker Club of which Tack is the leader.<br><br>What is the first thing Tyra sees upon getting out of her car at Ride? Tack kissing a tall, beautiful brunette goodbye. Whatever, Tyra needs this job. She’s been without one for too long. She’s going to do whatever it takes to survive.<br><br>Tack spots her and assumes that she’s there for him. But when she explains that she’s there for her first day of work, he informs her she can’t have the job because they’ve slept together. Tyra refuses to take this lying down and fights to keep her job. Tack states that if she’s in his bed again, she’s out the door. Then it’s on like Donkey Kong as Tack sets out to seduce her and Tyra is determined to resist.<br><br>Kristen Ashley books are really something special. She writes from a very honest place. Her characters resonate deep emotional truths that just plain ring true. She writes heroines who are so real. They are strong, beautiful, flawed, smart and always full of fire. Tyra was no exception. She had fears and insecurities but those were drowned out by how wonderful she was. So kind and accepting, with a heart of gold.<br><br>Tack has two teenage kids from a previous marriage that Tyra accepts and loves. Not because of their Dad, but because they are awesome kids and they earned it all on their own. She has layers and layers to her, all of them wonderful an fascinating. Tack sees this from the get go. <br><br>The way Tyra describes the effect Tack has had on her life, is that her world was black and white until she met him and brought color into her world. They are a fun pair to watch unfold. Tack being the tattooed, hawt, badass biker that makes pancakes and fajitas for his family and does anything he can to protect them, even from his ex-wife. And Tyra, the beautiful woman who decided long ago not to settle for anything less than her dream man, but when she finally finds him, it scares the bejeesus out of her. Tack is not without complications.<br><br>Tack and Tyra have amazing sexual chemistry and Tack is such a sexy dirty talker. It works. It works really well. The dialogue between the two becomes more and more intimate, as Tack is surprisingly sweet.<br><br>But their journey isn’t without outside strife. We have to deal with Tyra’s best friend and some trouble surrounding her, as well as problems with the Russian mob! But to sweeten an already great book, we get to see the other couples and Elvira (yay!) from the other books in the series a few times.<br><br>The magnificent Kristen Ashley does it again. Amazing characters, wonderful story, beautiful epilogue. Definite recommended read.<br><br><u>What I loved about Motorcycle Man:<u><br><br>*Tack calls Tyra “Red”, but won’t allow anyone else to call her that.<br>*Badass bikers with bigass hearts!<br>*Pepper spray smackdowns.<br>*KA’s descriptive writing. Nothing like it!<br>*Tattoos. Existing and proposed.<br>*Tabby and Rush. Great kids.<br>*How and why Tack checks for a pulse on the people he loves to reassure himself that they are ok.<br>*That Tack made Chaos not only run clean, but in the black. Giving it’s members a good life.<br>*Pizza and The Color Purple.<br>*Cherry Red 1967 Mustang Eleanor Fastback.<br>*The word “Greedy” has now become hot!<br>*Tack’s sweetness and Tyra’s inability to take it without crying.<br>*Dog tags for no reason.<br>*That Tack was willing to do whatever he had to to get his kids out of a bad situation from their home with their mother, Naomi.<br>*How Tyra dresses to come to work at a garage.<br>*The epilogue. Oh, how I love a Kristen Ashley epilogue.<br><br><u>What I didn’t love about Motorcycle Man:</u><br><br>*BeeBee the skank.<br>*That Tack was a bit of a jerk for a time. (This resolves.)<br>*The requirement of Tyra to turn a blind eye to someone’s cheating. I get it, but it feels like the sisterhood take a hit. And Kristen Ashley handles it with aplomb.<br><br><br>Here is a picture Kristen Ashley posted as having a Tack vibe.<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380371801i/724962.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Here is the playlist I made for Motorcycle Man using mostly youtube videos. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>"Red hair and black leather. My favorite color scheme." <br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=f_5Ean-VMUo&amp;feature=related" rel="nofollow noopener">1952 Vincent Black Lightening by Richard Thompson</a><br><br><a>Steppenwolf's Born to be Wild for the cross country trip.</a><br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=KRjUQXz2tyg" rel="nofollow noopener"> Don't fear the Reaper by Gus when Tack talks about finding his sister dead.</a><br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=SSf6-CGEOb8&amp;oref=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fresults%3Fsearch_query%3DPaula%2Bcole%26oq%3DPaula%2Bcole%26aq%3Df%26aqi%3Dg4%26aql%3D%26gs_l%3Dyoutube-reduced.3..0l4.82712.85779.0.85952.10.6.0.4.4.0.99.552.6.6.0...0.0.o3sRQFlIdwk&amp;has_verified=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Paula Cole's Feelin' Love for Tack and Red's Fuck-a-thon. (he makes her come 7 times and himself 3).</a><br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=EKZOStAWbQQ" rel="nofollow noopener">I like Apron Strings by Everything but the Girl, but I like this cover better. For when Tyra tells Tack She's pregnant.</a><br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Vppbdf-qtGU" rel="nofollow noopener"> ZZTop's The Grange for when Chaos and company go out and kick ass to get Tyra Back</a><br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=hvZKu3ZFg4k" rel="nofollow noopener">Hard Headed by Nic Cowan when Tyra is determined to not end up back in Tack's bed</a><br><br><a>Arms of a Woman by Amos Lee for the Epilogue – the last page really</a><br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=7F3hY0xJ-Jc&amp;feature=related" rel="nofollow noopener">Cover of Run to You by Driftplan and Toryn Green</a><br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=7hZsqL5ol5w" rel="nofollow noopener"> Sweet Sweet Baby by Michelle Featherstone for the sweet reconciles and Tyre’s inability to take Tack’s Sweetness</a> <br><br><a href="http://soundcloud.com/driftplan-1/02-grey" rel="nofollow noopener"> Grey by Driftplan because Tack gives her world color</a> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br></u></u></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_333530231" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/333530231" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/333530231?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer333530231" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7505702442959796440"><i> <b> “Life’s a roller coaster. Best damn ride in the park. You don’t close your eyes, hold on and wait for it to be over, babe. You keep your eyes open, lift your hands straight in the air and enjoy the ride for as long as it lasts.” </b></i> ~ Kane "Tack" Allen<br/><br/>A wonderful book with an amazing conclusion to a seriously badass series!<br/><br/>The last line of this book brought tears to my eyes. Boy does Ms. Ashley know how to write an epilogue!!<br/><br/>I absolutely adored how she brought ALL the characters that we have seen</span>
  <span id="freeText7505702442959796440" style="display:none"><i> <b> “Life’s a roller coaster. Best damn ride in the park. You don’t close your eyes, hold on and wait for it to be over, babe. You keep your eyes open, lift your hands straight in the air and enjoy the ride for as long as it lasts.” </b></i> ~ Kane "Tack" Allen<br /><br />A wonderful book with an amazing conclusion to a seriously badass series!<br /><br />The last line of this book brought tears to my eyes. Boy does Ms. Ashley know how to write an epilogue!!<br /><br />I absolutely adored how she brought ALL the characters that we have seen since the beginning of the series together. Throughout the whole series, they all help each other out here and there but in the finale of this book ALL the Alpha badasses joined forces and it was pretty freaking epic!!<br /><br /><i> <b> “We’ve hit the hot guy motherlode.” </b></i>  **SHIVERS**<br /><br />I loved Tyra! She was smart, sassy, sweet yet vulnerable, can-do, didn’t back down, and gave as good as she got. She was a fun heroine to read and definitely was the perfect match for her big badass biker.<br /><br />I’ve always liked Tack since we were first introduced to him in book 1, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12299419.Mystery_Man__Dream_Man___1_" title="Mystery Man (Dream Man, #1) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Mystery Man</a>, but the thing that made me fall in love with him was seeing the way he was around his kids and his family in his home life. Just absolutely melted my heart and left me grinning from ear to ear!<br /><br /><i> “I’m noticing a theme to Life with Kane Allen,” I remarked. <br />“Yeah, that theme is I got your back. I take care of you. You sleep easy. You eat good. And you feel safe. You tellin’ me you got a problem with that?” </i><br /><br />This book is also full of brilliant side characters. We see reoccurring ones like Elvira (who may be one of my fav female characters ever!) and also meet new ones like Tyra’s Aunt Bette and Uncle Marsh who were absolutely perfect, Tack’s kids Rush and Tabby whose stories I would love to read one day, Tack’s psycho ex-wife who was so crazy she actually had me laughing hysterically at times… not to mention the Russian mob and loads of badass bikers.<br /><br />I have to admit I had a few issues with this book. I didn’t like the appelations the bikers use for their significant others “old man” and “old lady” just really didn’t work for me and I inwardly cringed every time I read it. Also, I felt like there were points where Tack was too crude and too much of a jerk and his world not respectful of women enough for my taste. But that being said, he was hawt and he grew on me a lot, especially once they had the big ‘talk’ and we got to see his side of the story and what it was that had happened in his past to shape him into the man we all know as Tack. His behavior often had me saying "oh he did NOT just do/say that?!" but in the end, I felt he both grew as a person and redeemed himself. Together, he and Tyra found a beautiful compromise of their worlds :)<br /><br /><i> “I will be there in ten . And what I mean is, when I get there in ten, your ass better be there.”<br />Oh boy.<br />“Are you coming on your bike?”<br />“Yeah.”<br />“I’m in a tight, short, little acquamarine dress with high heels. I can’t get on a bike.”<br />“You’re in a tight, short dress and high heels?”<br />“Yes.”<br />“I’ll be there in five.” </i><br /><br />And his serious protectiveness of Tyra along with his no-bullshit attitude and unwillingness to let anything come between them stole my heart.<br /><br /><i>“You belong to Chaos. No one touches what belongs to Chaos. No one . They don’t touch it. They don’t hood it. They don’t bind it. They don’t even breathe in its space unless they have Chaos permission...<br />“I’m Chaos?”<br />“Was my dick just in you?”<br />I fought an annoyed growl and said, “Uh… yeah.”<br />“Then you’re Chaos.” </i><br /><br />See what I mean? Crude, but protective and kinda sweet lol.<br /><br />Seriously though, at the end, seeing Cabe “Hawk” Delgado, Brock Lucas, Mitch Lawson, and Kane “Tack” Allen working together gave me mega shivers!!! Kristen Ashley knows how to write EPIC BADASS at its finest! I actually SQUEED out loud when Hawk came on the page. I adore him! He is definitely my favorite of all the men even though I love them all <br /><br /><i>“… because Hawk, Brock and Mitch stormed that house at Tack’s side. This meant, to Tack, they were different kinds of brothers. Not of blood. Not of the cut. But that bond was unshakable all the same.” <br /><br />“Bottom line, no one fucks with my woman.” </i><br /><br />As with all the previous books from this series, the writing is smooth, fast paces, doesn’t drag, and keeps you flipping the pages. I read the book almost in one sitting despite it being a decent length.<br /><br />I absolutely can’t wait to read the spin-off biker series, Chaos, that will come next featuring Shy (serious swoon material!!) and Tack’s daughter Tabby.<br /><br /><br />Also, if you have already read Motorcycle Man, this is a great little link by Kristen Ashley to read (but spoilers if you haven’t read it): <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author_blog_posts/2489327-middle-ground#comment_51169838" rel="nofollow noopener">Middle Ground </a><br /><br />For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br /><br />And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="7505702442959796440" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_354497375" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/354497375" />
    <a title="Arlene" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene"><img alt="Arlene" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1347048609p2/1746727.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/354497375?book_show_action=true">Jun 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arlene" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arlene" href="/user/show/1746727-arlene">Arlene</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Arlene by: </span>
      Smut Monday Club
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1746727-arlene?shelf=read-2012">read-2012</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer354497375" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8261627081367296794"><b>Rating Clarification:</b> 1.5 Star (but I'm just bumping it to 2)<br/><br/><b>Motorcycle Man</b> is the first book I’ve read by Kristen Ashley and I think that’s where I went wrong. I probably should have read books 1 – 3 in this series in order to get an initial impression or appreciation for the main character Tack. So meeting him for the first time in <b>Motorcycle Man</b> was a bit of a shocker for me. <br/><br/>I would rate Tack a 15 on the alpha man scale of 1 – 10. Don’t get me wrong, I like alphas but they have to deliver th</span>
  <span id="freeText8261627081367296794" style="display:none"><b>Rating Clarification:</b> 1.5 Star (but I'm just bumping it to 2)<br /><br /><b>Motorcycle Man</b> is the first book I’ve read by Kristen Ashley and I think that’s where I went wrong. I probably should have read books 1 – 3 in this series in order to get an initial impression or appreciation for the main character Tack. So meeting him for the first time in <b>Motorcycle Man</b> was a bit of a shocker for me. <br /><br />I would rate Tack a 15 on the alpha man scale of 1 – 10. Don’t get me wrong, I like alphas but they have to deliver their strength with a bit of finesse or a sporadic gentle caress in order for me to fall for their character. Tack was befitting of his name… he was just too sharp and rough around the edges for me all around, and I just couldn’t come to like him much. The way he talked, the way he treated Tyra, it was all too harsh and too much for me.<br /><br />Typically, I give books a 1 star if I couldn’t finish it and 2 stars if I didn’t like. For this book, I read the first 200 ePages and then skipped to the last 75 ePages. However, I’m still giving it an extra half star because frankly I’m actually hesitant to even give it such a low rating to begin with considering all of the glowing reviews for this book. Part of me thinks I missed out on something special, something great and I’m bummed I didn’t care for it as much as other readers did. But, I think I can attribute it to the fact that the protag and the writing didn’t fit my style.<br /><br />Ashley’s writing style takes a lot of patience for me to handle. I feel she repeats herself too much, where I read through a few pages with the same conversation going back and forth leaving me feeling like I’ve accomplished nothing. I mean let’s take the sandwich scene for example:<br />Tack: <i>Red go get me a sandwich</i><br />Red: <i>Whaaa???</i><br />Tack: <i>Red, I’m hungry go get me a sandwich</i><br />Red: <i>You want me to get you a whaaaa???</i><br />Tack: <i>Listen, I said I want a sandwich. You’re in my world. So when I say I want a sandwich, you go and do it.</i><br />Red: <i>Wait, so you’re standing there telling me I should…</i><br />Tack: <i>Go get me a sandwich.</i><br /><br />Okay, in my head I’m screaming GO.GET.YOUR.OWN.DAME.SANDWICH and other stuff too, but I don’t want my angry girl hormones to reveal themselves. Oh and I sort of adlibbed that little convo, but believe me, I’m pretty close to the actual thing. Even Tyra’s narrative felt very repetitious and I found myself losing my patience more than once.<br /><br />Overall, I’m bummed I didn’t come to like this book as the reviews and reactions seemed promising. I think Kristen Ashley just might not be for me. Oh well I come across that every now and again...</span>
  <a data-text-id="8261627081367296794" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer289325063" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18244736513848252981"><i>"5-I'm livin' my life in colour for the first time Stars!"</i><br/><br/>This is my fourth read of this book, and it was like I was reading it for the first time. <br/>You see, it has been 3 years since I last visited Tack and Tyra and I had forgotten how much I loved their chemistry and the dynamics of their characters.<br/><br/>The characters, writing, and story were amazing, and in true KA fashion- she gave her readers a kick-ass epilogue.<br/><br/>5 ++<br/>AMAZING story and I'm sorry the series has to end... but OH WHAT A GREAT ENDING!</span>
  <span id="freeText18244736513848252981" style="display:none"><i>"5-I'm livin' my life in colour for the first time Stars!"</i><br><br>This is my fourth read of this book, and it was like I was reading it for the first time. <br>You see, it has been 3 years since I last visited Tack and Tyra and I had forgotten how much I loved their chemistry and the dynamics of their characters.<br><br>The characters, writing, and story were amazing, and in true KA fashion- she gave her readers a kick-ass epilogue.<br><br>5 ++<br>AMAZING story and I'm sorry the series has to end... but OH WHAT A GREAT ENDING!!!<br>Tack and Tyra are AMAZING together!<br>Loved the story, the writing, and another FRIGGIN AWESOME Epilogue! *sigh*<br><br>CAN NOT WAIT TO READ THE CHAOS SERIES!! Tabby stole my heart and Shy... well Shy will be interesting to read when He gives his heart away.<br><br><b>
  <i>Second read: Oct 11-12, 2012<br> <br> This was so much better the second read, because even though I knew the story and the outcome... I felt I had more time to savour the characters and the story. I did, however, feel it was along the lines of "Sons of Anarchy" (which isn't bad because I'm a huge fan and Charlie Hunman *sigh*)<br><br> ... again LOVED Tack &amp; Tyra together. When they loved they loved deep, true and their passion was off the charts with nothing held back.<br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/albums/i477/hebbies37/?action=view&amp;current=hotkiss.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380371602i/724737.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><br>I really enjoyed Rush &amp; Tabby (Tack's children) this time around because I paid more attention to their characters.<br><br>Nothing has changed in my rating (still a 5 ++) <br>If you like reading about kick-ass, dominate, uber-alpha biker bad-ass males who walk on the dark side, but are trying to find some light.... then you'll LOVE this story! </i>
</b><br><br><br><u>Third read: August 11-12, 2014</u><br><br>The above rating still applies. LOVED IT!!<br>Tack and Tyra are still sizzling, hot!<br><br><a href="http://s1095.photobucket.com/user/hebbies37/media/review%20pics%20for%20me/http3A2F2F24.media.tumblr.com2F40a7e923428c80d9df658614e0c5a8842Ftumblr_n6njz5dTmG1rum7cgo1_1280.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3527738063?book_show_action=true">Sep 01, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arini" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arini" href="/user/show/39722464-arini">Arini</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3527738063" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3671917553784930168">#3 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3501049592?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Law Man</a> — 4.25 Stars<br/>#4 Motorcycle Man — 4.5 Stars<br/><br/><i>When in doubt, go read (listen to) a KA book . . . </i><br/><br/>I loved this! 😭 The plot was more prominent in here compare to the previous book (which I liked), but the romance was just as wholesome. There was a hassle with an OW and Tack’s ex wife, but honestly I think it added flavor to the story. While it may be annoying, it was also hilarious and the culmination of it resulted in some emotional moments between Tack and Tyra (which I appreciated).<br/><br/>Tyra w</span>
  <span id="freeText3671917553784930168" style="display:none">#3 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3501049592?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Law Man</a> — 4.25 Stars<br />#4 Motorcycle Man — 4.5 Stars<br /><br /><i>When in doubt, go read (listen to) a KA book . . . </i><br /><br />I loved this! 😭 The plot was more prominent in here compare to the previous book (which I liked), but the romance was just as wholesome. There was a hassle with an OW and Tack’s ex wife, but honestly I think it added flavor to the story. While it may be annoying, it was also hilarious and the culmination of it resulted in some emotional moments between Tack and Tyra (which I appreciated).<br /><br />Tyra was fire! Though I did wish sometimes she’d just unleash it and go head to head with Tack without being the first one to cave in. Tack was different from Mitch (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13412515.Law_Man__Dream_Man___3_" title="Law Man (Dream Man, #3) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">Law Man</a>) but still as dreamy. 🙈 He was good and bad and everything in between. I adored Rush and Tabby (Tack’s teenage children) and their get to know moments with Tyra. The MC background was the cherry on top.<br /><br />My frustration (still) came from the writing, which in true KA fashion (tedious and repetitive) also had the addictive effect in full force. It drove me crazy that she’d go off topic to be overly descriptive about unimportant sh*t (kinda reminded me of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5760202.Mariana_Zapata" title="Mariana Zapata" rel="nofollow noopener">Mariana Zapata</a>). I think part of the reason my KA reads have been a success so far is because I read them all on audio in which the narration to me was just flawless. 👌👌<br /><br /><b>
  <i>(Read as an Audiobook)</i>
</b></span>

<div id="review_1444993897" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1444993897" />
    <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four"><img alt="Robin (Bridge Four)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473392517p2/14105531.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1444993897?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/21883167-motorcycle-man">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=bro-mantic">bro-mantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=adorable-alphas">adorable-alphas</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=chocolate-pms-day-reads">chocolate-pms-day-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=cotton-candy">cotton-candy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=book-boyfriend-material">book-boyfriend-material</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=4-5-stars">4-5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=sexy">sexy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1444993897" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1933524774063723968"><b>Sale Alert: Kindle Daily Deal May 4 <a href='https://www.amazon.com/dp/B00AHFJACM/ref=s9_acsd_al_bw_c2_x_7_i?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=merchandised-search-2&pf_rd_r=RVBGDQYEKQF2GWZ21KP1&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=cc8c0b0c-a5bb-4644-83fb-c0dc74227daa&pf_rd_i=11552285011' rel='nofollow noopener'>$1.99</a></b><br/>Buddy Read with my fellow KA-Land Loving Girls at <a>Buddies Books and Baubles</a><br/><br/><b>Have you ever noticed that the line between alpha man and total douchebag is really blurry?</b> It is amazing to me that in KA-land I just accept the heroes so completely when usually in the beginning they start out a bit on the side of douchebaggery and then slowly shift to hot alpha man that I can love forever.<br/><br/>This is not different for Tack, he starts this book clearly on the side of</span>
  <span id="freeText1933524774063723968" style="display:none"><b>Sale Alert: Kindle Daily Deal May 4 <a href="https://www.amazon.com/dp/B00AHFJACM/ref=s9_acsd_al_bw_c2_x_7_i?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_s=merchandised-search-2&amp;pf_rd_r=RVBGDQYEKQF2GWZ21KP1&amp;pf_rd_t=101&amp;pf_rd_p=cc8c0b0c-a5bb-4644-83fb-c0dc74227daa&amp;pf_rd_i=11552285011" rel="nofollow noopener">$1.99</a></b><br />Buddy Read with my fellow KA-Land Loving Girls at <a>Buddies Books and Baubles</a><br /><br /><b>Have you ever noticed that the line between alpha man and total douchebag is really blurry?</b> It is amazing to me that in KA-land I just accept the heroes so completely when usually in the beginning they start out a bit on the side of douchebaggery and then slowly shift to hot alpha man that I can love forever.<br /><br />This is not different for Tack, he starts this book clearly on the side of grade A first class asshole. Tyra met Tack and knew right away he was the man for her. Unfortunately Tack did not feel the same way, to him she was just another great lay in a long line of great lays. <b> So what was special to Tyra from the beginning was just another tequila induced sex-a-thon to Tack. Until she shows him the sass.</b><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“So you’re good-looking, have great tats and a cool goatee. So you caught my eye and I caught yours. <b>We had sex. Lots of sex. It was good. So what? That was then, this is now. We’re not going to play, not again. We’re done playing.</b> I’m going to come in at eight, leave at five, do my job, and you’re going to be my scary biker dude boss, sign my paychecks, do my performance evaluations and maybe, if you’re nice, I’ll make you coffee. Other than that, you don’t exist for me and I don’t exist for you. <b>What we had, we had. It’s over.</b> I’m moving on and how I’m moving on is, I’m… working… this… job.”</i>
</blockquote><br />She might has well waved a red flag in front of the bull because what do alpha men on the douchebag side of the line like more than sass is a straight up challenge. Tyra just declared she was a challenge and now Tack is going to make sure he conquers that gauntlet that she has just thrown down.<br /><br />I don’t really know anything about motorcycle clubs and the men in them but this was a pretty good and semi-tame intro to that world. The idea of brothers and going to the mat for all the men in your crew I definitely liked. Tack becomes great as a love interest even if he started a little on the wrong side of the douchebag line. It is soon that we get the soft belly underneath the hard badass exterior. <br /><blockquote>
  <i>”… I figure I’d find my way to beauty eventually. And I’d find absolution because I’d know, I earned the love of that woman, a woman who’s got so much to her it’ll take years to dig down and find the heart of her, that would be my reward.”</i>
</blockquote><br />I love living in KA-Land where hot alpha men run rampant and there is always a touch of drama and pain with the joy and the hilarity of some of the situations. Motorcycle Man is filled with a great blend of these.<br /><blockquote>✔ - Semi Drunk Girl scene full of hilarity with the girls. Drunken Tyra is pretty funny when she freaks out.<br />✔ - 2 yes count them <b>2</b> abductions (I don’t care I love those) <br />✔ - Cameos from all the Dream Men *fans self*<br />✔ - Crazy Family/Best Friend drama<br />✔ - An Aunt with some unexpected Skills<br />✔ - Elvira doing cute babytalk to a future badass commando<br />✔ - Alpha mannerism that annoying at first turns out to be incredibly and adorably sweet. A man can put his hand on my throat anytime if it means what it means to Tack.<br />✔ - Showdown with the Russian Mob.</blockquote><br />Add all that together and it is totally a great time in the making. I liked Tyra more than some of the other KA heroines and let’s face it she did not stand a chance against the onslaught when Tack decided she would be his. But it was fun to watch her make him work for it.<br /><br />This was a great conclusion to the Dream Man series. But I’m incredibly happy that there is more Chaos and Tack in the Chaos series. I’m now ready to take a walk into the world of Motorcycle clubs and the badass alphas that live in that world.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13673731835202437294"><b>A perfect ending for a fabulous series! One of the best KA books so far. <br/>5 stars is just not good enough!</b><br/><br/><br/><b>The story</b> - great! Tack was being a jerk at the beginning (kinda like Hawk XD), and then he just kept getting sweeter <a href='http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&current=767622.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText13673731835202437294" style="display:none"><b>A perfect ending for a fabulous series! One of the best KA books so far. <br>5 stars is just not good enough!</b><br><br><br><b>The story</b> - great! Tack was being a jerk at the beginning (kinda like Hawk XD), and then he just kept getting sweeter <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=767622.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/362324.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> First refusing to hire her, then refusing to fire her XD And when he came with the pizza and they watched movies <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=3402580550.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/362254.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> one of the best scenes EVER! It was lovely to watch them falling in love &lt;3 And of course as in all the best KA-s, there was a big action scene in the end (God I hated that, very difficult to read), and of course as in all the best KA-s, the epilogue made me cry <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=815594.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/348723.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> &lt;3 beautiful &lt;3<br><br><br><b>Tyra</b> - awsome! I just love the fact that she can't have any conversation with Tack that doesn't end up with them fighting (bickering actually XD) It was just fun to read <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=biggestgrin_zps92d5aecd.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/372503.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> She is not used to men like Tack, she doesn't get his signals, so they have their ups and downs pretty often XD She was awsome when she kicked Tabby's boyfriend's ass!! <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=3079029344.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/371936.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> And later Naomi hahahah A great character!<br><br><br><b>Tack</b> - <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=72866.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/362766.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=787264.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/372534.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=3402580550.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/362254.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a>! In the KA world, I think Tack goes in the alpha-caveman-badass-emotional category XD This is a guy who does what he wants, when he wants it, how he wants it, no matter what. Being a biker dude - automatic hotness! Tatoo-s all over him - hotness! Goatee - HOT-NESS! But even though he's tough and badass, he has a sweet side that he showes Tyra when she lets him in &lt;3 Loved that &lt;3 and the fact that he figured out Tyra is the one for him, so no matter what happens, he'd never let her go &lt;3 mush all over <a href="http://s977.photobucket.com/albums/ae254/Black_Morena/Emoticons/?action=view&amp;current=908279.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374019ra/727910.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><br>And here's a pic I stole (sorry) from another review, just fell in love with it &lt;3 It's totally Tack and Tyra &lt;3 beautiful :)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380739425i/3117595.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Old review: <br><br>Well this was just fabulous, I LOVED the whole book, it deserves a 10 star rating! I looked forward to reading about Tack from the first book, and this one didn't dissapoint me :) As always, full of emotions, the ending was intense, and I'm kinda sad the Dream Man series is over :( Although I must say, Elvira is my favotite KA character so far, I wish she got a book of her own :)</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/975772349" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/975772349?book_show_action=true">Jun 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=books-that-deserve-more-than-five-s">books-that-deserve-more-than-five-s</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer975772349" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16355974601043243272">*****5+++++++ You Colored My World Stars*****<br/>(BR with Melissa, Dee, Tiffany, and Kelli)<br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/4e6fe24d19b13512b5f5c42deb82aeb8_zps66509229.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403885853i/10157893._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 4e6fe24d19b13512b5f5c42deb82aeb8_zps66509229.jpg' width='375' height='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><b>"Motorcycle Man"</b>, is definitely my <b>FAVE</b> out of the <u>
  <b>"Dream Man"</b>
</u> series.<br/>AND, Tack, he's My <b>#1 KA ALPHA</b>!!!!<br/>Hmmm, dare I say it????<br/><b>YES!!</b> He's my <b>#1 BAD ASS MC BIKER</b>!!!<br/><br/><br/>This book reeled me in from the beginning and it never let go!<br/>I was in complete book heaven!!<br/>Tyra Masters aka "Red", is a 35 year old woman, whose decided her life needs some shaking up.<br/>She's led a pretty dull life and has never been one to d</span>
  <span id="freeText16355974601043243272" style="display:none">*****5+++++++ You Colored My World Stars*****<br>(BR with Melissa, Dee, Tiffany, and Kelli)<br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/4e6fe24d19b13512b5f5c42deb82aeb8_zps66509229.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403885853i/10157893._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4e6fe24d19b13512b5f5c42deb82aeb8_zps66509229.jpg" width="375" height="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>"Motorcycle Man"</b>, is definitely my <b>FAVE</b> out of the <u>
  <b>"Dream Man"</b>
</u> series.<br>AND, Tack, he's My <b>#1 KA ALPHA</b>!!!!<br>Hmmm, dare I say it????<br><b>YES!!</b> He's my <b>#1 BAD ASS MC BIKER</b>!!!<br><br><br>This book reeled me in from the beginning and it never let go!<br>I was in complete book heaven!!<br>Tyra Masters aka "Red", is a 35 year old woman, whose decided her life needs some shaking up.<br>She's led a pretty dull life and has never been one to do anything spontaneous, but Tyra is sick of the "same old", and the toxic people that surround her, so spontaneity lands her a job as the new office manager at <b>"Ride Custom Cars and Bikes"</b> and also in the bed of one SINFULLY SEXY, Kane "Tack" Allen!!!!<br><br><br><br>Tyra is seeing an "HEA" with Tack, after their first night of HOT sex together, but Tack is seeing her as a one night stand, and basically telling her - <i>"Don't let the door hit your ass on your way out."</i><br>Tyra's a truly amazing heroine. <br>She has a heart of gold, but is also quite feisty, and can stand up to big, BAD TACK!!!<br>He becomes completely mesmerized by Tyra, with every little piece of herself that she reveals to him over time.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/548d3562f9a1702226d14c15be33a91e_zps9b5d2a98.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403885853i/10157894._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 548d3562f9a1702226d14c15be33a91e_zps9b5d2a98.jpg" width="375" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Tack and Tyra have a rough start in the beginning, but it's Tack who see's he may have misjudged Tyra, and he pursues her hard. You might even say he did a bit of <b>"wooing"</b>, in his own sinfully delicious way!!<br><br><br>I fell really HARD for this man.<br>He was gorgeous, extremely ALPHA, sexually insatiable, but MOST of all, he <b>LOVED</b> with everything he had in his heart! Which was <b>ENORMOUS</b>!<br>Tack isn't into playing games, and he is a man who appreciates a woman who has a bit of "SOFT" inside her.<br><br><br>I've noticed with most of the books in this series, that I relate to the heroine. There are pieces of me that I have in common with each of them. <br>I loved that she had a picture of her "dream man" and that she was never going to settle for anything less.<br>Why should we settle for less???!!<br>I think we all deserve the man of our dreams with an HEA to top all HEAs!!!!!<br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I promised myself, as a little girl, that I would settle for nothing less than my dream man. Nothing less. It was crazy. I've thought on it and I don't even know why I vowed that to myself, I just did. Girls do that, sure. Then the reality of life seeps in and they get over it. My dream man or nothing. So I looked for him my whole life. I was going to live that dream, I would settle for nothing less. So I had nothing until that night at Ride when I met you."</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/938cf443714e2085a225b80eab988ff6_zps5a460b38.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1403920249i/10164801._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 938cf443714e2085a225b80eab988ff6_zps5a460b38.jpg" width="375" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This story has a bunch of awesome secondary characters.<br>Loved Tabby and Rush. Can't wait to read their stories!!<br>Well,I'm hoping that Rush gets one!<br>Aunt Bette and Uncle Marshall were Kick Ass and Uncle Marshall definitely had me in tears during one of his conversations with Tyra.<br><br><br>We get all of our other Dream Men, their women, and Elvira!!<br>Always love catching up with them and we do get plenty of them in this book!!<br>There's heart pounding action as well!!<br><br><br>I am so happy that I finally got around to reading KA's books and that I got to experience this one with some of the most wonderful book buddies ever!!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16355974601043243272" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        rated it

              <span id="reviewTextContainer275543337" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8756895083335449962"><b>
  <i>ALRIGHT!!!! I'm gonna swear, so if anyone gets offended by this, PLEASE STOP READING NOW!!!</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>BEST FUCKING BOOK IN THE HISTORY OF KRISTEN ASHLEY BOOKS!!!!</b> You know i was waiting forever for Tack's story and boy, did this story exceed every one of my expectations!!! I LOVED everything about Tack, his tatts, his bike, his mind, his goatee... but oh mostly his dirty, dirty mouth!!!! Seriously he could use that mouth on me ANYTIME and ANYWHERE on my body, if he so wanted!!! *drool* And i must admit</span>
  <span id="freeText8756895083335449962" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>ALRIGHT!!!! I'm gonna swear, so if anyone gets offended by this, PLEASE STOP READING NOW!!!</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>BEST FUCKING BOOK IN THE HISTORY OF KRISTEN ASHLEY BOOKS!!!!</b> You know i was waiting forever for Tack's story and boy, did this story exceed every one of my expectations!!! I LOVED everything about Tack, his tatts, his bike, his mind, his goatee... but oh mostly his dirty, dirty mouth!!!! Seriously he could use that mouth on me ANYTIME and ANYWHERE on my body, if he so wanted!!! *drool* And i must admit, i did not like Tyra much at the start, but i got it in the end... i got her... <b>AND THE BEST SCENE EVER</b> was Tack, Hawk, Brock, Mitch and OMG OMG OMG Hector in the bar!!!!!!! *SQUEAL* hello HOT FANTASY!!!<br /><br /><b>AND BEST FUCKING EPILOGUE EVER!!!</b> You know i've ALWAYS said in my reviews that your epilogues are the BOMB, and this one was no exception!!! And *SQUEAL* <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[a SPINOFF????!!!! about Tabitha and Sky... that is going to be FREAKIN' EPIC!!! I already want to read their story NOW!!! LOL! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />You know i've loved your work for a long time now Kristen, BUT i will admit, i haven't been able to fully get into your last couple of books (no fault of your own... just personal taste and all) BUT, Motorcycle Man for me is back to PURE KA!!! Without a doubt this is the BEST BOOK in the Dream Man series and Tack now ranks up there for me in <b>KRISTEN ASHLEY MCHOTTIE HEAVEN</b>... i think he still comes in after Ty and Hector (you KNOW how much i love Ty and Hector and still have dreams about them and wanna have their babies), BUT he's leapfrogged in front of Tate and Gray!!!<br /><br />*SIGH*... in conclusion, read the damn book people because you are going to FREAKIN' LOVE IT!!!</span>

<div id="review_890217340" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/890217340" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/890217340?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2014">read-in-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer890217340" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12693566723657274291">We finally get to Tack's story...the guy we've been reading about since the first book, <i>Dream Man</i>. He didn't get the girl in that book and while of course, he gets the girl in this book, will she be woman enough for the badass biker? <br/><br/>I have to admit, Tack really didn't win me over...<i>at first</i>. He's such a typical KA Alpha and extremely forceful. Poor Tyra didn't know what in the heck was going on most of the time! But slowly as we get to know Tack better, we find out things that can only endear h</span>
  <span id="freeText12693566723657274291" style="display:none">We finally get to Tack's story...the guy we've been reading about since the first book, <i>Dream Man</i>. He didn't get the girl in that book and while of course, he gets the girl in this book, will she be woman enough for the badass biker? <br><br>I have to admit, Tack really didn't win me over...<i>at first</i>. He's such a typical KA Alpha and extremely forceful. Poor Tyra didn't know what in the heck was going on most of the time! But slowly as we get to know Tack better, we find out things that can only endear him to you. <br><br>Tyra is also a typical KA female. She's at a bit of a loss and trying to make her life better. She sees Tack and immediately lets him take her to bed. She believes he is her Dream Man. Only problem is Tack kicks her out of his bed when he's done with her! Unbeknownst to Tack, Tyra is his new office manager and when he finds out, he doesn't want her there. But Tyra holds her ground and that keeps Tack intrigued. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1391151014i/8336747._SY540_.png" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you've been reading the series, you know there's been things going on with the Russians. Things come to a head and poor Tyra is involved on two fronts. The good thing is we get all the prior characters being involved and I loved that. <br><br>We also have to deal with Tack's ex wife and she is a handful! I liked how Tyra handled her and I <i>really</i> liked what she didn't get in the end. <br><br>Through all this, Tyra and Tack try to make a go at a relationship. Sometimes it works and sometimes Tyra tries to end it but Tack will have nothing to do with that! <br><br>As per usual KA style, there are some steamy scenes. Hearing about Tyra being "greedy" made me giggle. I also like how realistic they were with the kids in the house. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396049228i/9082841._SY540_.png" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There's a part towards the end that is pretty tear worthy. I really liked how Gwen was there for Tack...<i>with</i> Hawke's encouragement. And I loved the dog tags. <br><br>I also really enjoyed Tack's kids, Tabby and Rush and I'm really excited to read Tabby's book in the Chaos series especially since Shy seems really yummy! Hopefully there will be a Rush book too. <br><br>Speaking of the Chaos series, the second book, <i>Fire Inside</i>, is about Lanie, Tyra's best friend. She goes through some rough stuff in this book but I was really shocked who she's supposed to be with in the Chaos book! <br><br><br><b>
  <u>Recommendation:</u>
</b><br><br>Obviously, if you're a Kristen Ashley fan you will love this. And if you're a motorcycle club fan you will love this. But if you want a good love story with an Alpha male and some drama, then you'll <i>really</i> love this.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396049661i/9082899.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ “He’s unlike any man I’ve ever met. He takes bossy to an extreme. I’ve never experienced anything like it.”<br><br>♥ “She’s dark, you’re red. I’ll fuck dark, I’ll fuck sun but only red has staying power. Considered sun once. Lost her. Now it’s you.”<br><br>♥ “Clue in, Red. What I’m tellin’ you is that you are not pullin’ shit over on me. I’m a biker but I’m not an idiot. You entered this game, you knew it was a game and you made the decision, conscious or unconscious, to play it with me. And you’re playin’ it with me."<br><br>♥ “Every day, somethin’ new. Will I ever get to the heart of you?”<br><br>♥ “Fuck me, she really can’t handle sweet,” he muttered to the ceiling. <br><br>“So stop doing it,” I suggested. <br><br>“Not a chance,” he returned."<br><br>♥ “I do,” I gasped. “I like everything about you, honey. Everything. Lived in black and white seems like all my life. Never noticed. Not until you colored my world.”<br><br>♥ “What I will not accept is being shoved against the wall, a car or even a pillow with your hand at my throat.” <br><br>To this, he replied immediately, “But your pulse is there, baby.”<br><br>♥ “Let me get this straight. Did you just accept my non-marriage offer?” <br><br>“Non-marriage?”<br><br>“I didn’t ask!” My voice was rising. <br><br>“So you just wanna shack up?” he asked but didn’t wait on my answer. “I’m good with that too.” <br><br>Gah! “I’m getting my huge-ass wedding,” I declared. <br><br>“So you are askin’ me to marry you,” he noted.<br><br>♥ “Babe, you can declare all you want. That don’t mean I’ll let you walk out on me.” <br><br>My lungs quit working. <br><br>“Never let you go,” Tack went on."<br><br>♥ “Don’t let me go,” she whispered. <br>“I won’t let you go, Red.” <br>“Don’t let me go.” <br>“I won’t let you go, baby.” <br>“Don’t let me go.”<br> <br>♥ “You don’t know this, baby, but some men have dream women too.”</span>
  <a data-text-id="12693566723657274291" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Rjm39dW3yy3DBlCD7ki4+g60awk3pvxBt/Oyib/OJlRYMQ8ChdRcRvG4xFkPM2npXZKA9NFW7X0m87X/pDkpOw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5LLKhB9jEmDFRkby2EcsO6KhHRI2DnZdJVPIIyD3/wf6unJzTwCFC/f40ig5PP0o8Yf279D+Z2G0U89VOwDwaA==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText4512985235668296011" style="display:none">Kristen Ashley was born in Gary, Indiana, USA. She nearly killed her mother and herself making it into the world, seeing as she had the umbilical cord wrapped around her neck (already attempting to accessorise and she hadn't taken her first breath!). <br /><br />Kristen grew up in Brownsburg, Indiana but has lived in Denver, Colorado and the West Country of England. Thus she has been blessed to have friends and family around the globe. Her posse is loopy (to say the least) but loopy is good when you want to write.<br /><br />Kristen was raised in a house with a large and multi-generational family. They lived on a very small farm in a small town in the heartland and existed amongst the strains of Glenn Miller, The Everly Brothers, REO Speedwagon and Whitesnake (and the wardrobes that matched).<br /><br />Needless to say, growing up in a house full of music, clothes and love was a good way to grow up. <br /><br />And as she keeps growing up, it keeps getting better.</span>
